| callingusername | string  | Username of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserName.                                                | Commonly used in detection  |
| callinguid      | string  | User ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserSid.                                                  |                             |
| callinglogonid  | string  | Windows login ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectLogonId.                                         |                             |
| targetdomain    | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetDomainName.                                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection |
| targetusername  | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetUserName.                                                                                        | Commonly used in detection  |
| targetlogonid   | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetLogonId.                                                                                         |                             |

--- Table End ---

Common Taxonomy and Metaclass Usage
Metaclass Definitions
Classes in the Helix taxonomy represent types of events or log sources. A metaclass is simply a generic class name that refers to events from one or more actual classes in Helix.

--- Table Start ---

| Metaclass       | Description                                                                                                                                                                           |
|---|---|
| antivirus       | Events generated by AV or similar host-based mechanisms (ClamAV, Symantec, Sophos, McAfee, etc.)                                                                                      |
| app_transaction | Any application based transaction activity to include application, database, or similar API transaction record                                                                        |
| auth            | Events pertaining to authentication or authorization (SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc.)                                                                                 |
| cloud           | Events pertaining to cloud infrastructure and services                                                                                                                                |
| connection      | Connection based events providing visibility of network protocols (netflow, sflow, jflow, session, connection, etc.)                                                                  |
| dhcp            | Events pertaining to Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and IP address allocation                                                                                             |
| dlp             | Events pertaining to Data Loss Prevention (DLP) or related practices                                                                                                                  |
| dns             | Events referring to any method or transaction used to interact with DNS records                                                                                                       |
| email           | Events pertaining to email message transfer (SMTP or similar logs)                                                                                                                    |
| file_xfer       | File transfers in any protocol (FTP, HTTP, SMB, BitTorrent, etc.)                                                                                                                     |
| firewall        | Connection accept/deny events generated by firewalls or similar devices which enforce ACLs on network traffic (VLAN, ACLs, etc.)                                                      |
| health          | Specialized events providing health metrics of a sensor or server                                                                                                                     |
| http_proxy      | Outbound web browsing events processed by an HTTP proxy. Includes events generated by other sources with similar content handling outgoing HTTP traffic                               |
| http_server     | Inbound web request events to a hosted web server.  Includes events generated by other sources with similar content (apache, nginx, firewalls, reverse proxies, load balancers, etc.) |
| ids             | Intrusion detection/prevention system alerts, including network (Snort, Suricata, Bro) or host-based (McAfee HIPS, OSSEC) alerts                                                      |
| nat             | Network address translation events (NAT or PAT)                                                                                                                                       |
| posix           | Events originating from POSIX, Unix, and Linux based services                                                                                                                         |
| privilege       | Events that indicate escalated user privileges(Cisco enable, sudo, runas, Windows impersonation, etc.)                                                                                |
| vpn             | VPN events from either site-to-site VPN tunnels or end user client-access VPN events                                                                                                  |
| vulnerability   | Events pertaining to vulnerability management, penetration testing, and related practices                                                                                             |
| windows         | Microsoft Windows events originating from any service in use on domain controller or workstation                                                                                      |

--- Table End ---

Commonly Used Taxonomy
General Event Information
Commonly used in many types of events.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type      | Description                                                                         | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid        | string    | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier             | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtime      | date-time | date/time that the actual event took place, as found in the payload of the message. | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtype      | string    | Type of event                                                                       | Commonly used in detection |
| msg            | string    | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Alert & Malware Information
Typically alerts from FireEye or other security products. These events may be of the antivirus or ids metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                              | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| action         | string | Action in the generic sense, typically representing action taken as a result of an event (allow, drop, quarantine, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |
| category       | string | General purpose field for Category, typically identifies a product specific category of event, alert, or activity        | Commonly used in detection |
| severity       | string | General purpose field used to capture severity level                                                                     | Commonly used in detection |
| virus          | string | General purpose field for representing the vendor specified streetname for a virus.                                      | Commonly used in detection |
| malwarename    | string | Used to represent the name of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |
| malwaretype    | string | Used to represent the type of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Network Connections
Network connections may be detailed in a variety of events including those of the connection, firewall, and http_proxy metaclasses.
Parsing should prioritize primary source and destination information including IP addresses that can be used in intel and analytics.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                          | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the source host      | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the source host      | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| srchost        | string  | Hostname of the source host          | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| srcport        | integer | Source port number                   | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| dstipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the destination host | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                      |
| dstipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the destination host | Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| dsthost        | string  | Hostname of the destination host     |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| dstport        | integer | Destination port number              | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |

--- Table End ---

VPN Connections
VPN connections should be parsed similar to other types network connections. Parsing should prioritize user and source IP/host information that can be used to detect abnormal logons. These events should be of the vpn metaclass, although it is not necessary for analytics.
HTTP Requests
HTTP requests are typically seen in events from HTTP proxies, servers, or other L7 network devices. These events should be of the http_proxy or http_server metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                          | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. May be extracted from url. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| uri            | string  | Full URI of a resource. May be extracted from url.                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| httpmethod     | string  | HTTP method (GET, POST, PUT, etc.)                                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| statuscode     | integer | HTTP status code (200, 404, 500, etc.)                                                               | Commonly used in detection                        |
| useragent      | string  | HTTP user agent string.                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |
| referrer       | string  | HTTP referrer header.                                                                                | Commonly used in detection                        |
| clientvars     | string  | Client header variables                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

DNS Requests
DNS requests are typically seen in events from DNS servers or L7 network devices. These events should be of the dns metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                               | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| querytype      | integer | A QTYPE value specifying the type of query (1, 2, 6, 12, 28, etc.)        | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| querytypename  | string  | A descriptive name for the type of query (A, NS, SOA, PTR, AAAA, etc.)    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| protocol       | string  | Protocol used in a session (http, ftp, smtp, etc.)                        | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

File Transfers
File transfers via HTTP, FTP, SMB, etc. These events should be of the file_xfer metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                                                  | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| filename       | string | General purpose field for storing a file name. May or may not include the full file path.                                                                                    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| filepath       | string | General purpose field for storing a file path.                                                                                                                               | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| hash           | string | General purpose field for storing any type of message digest hash value. Use when hashing algorithm is unknown or inconsistent. Otherwise, use md5, sha1, or sha256 instead. |                                                   |
| md5            | string | Computed MD5 hash of an object                                                                                                                                               | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha1           | string | Computed SHA1 hash of an object                                                                                                                                              | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha256         | string | Computed SHA256 hash of an object                                                                                                                                            | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| size           | string | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                                                                             | Sometimes used in detection                       |

--- Table End ---

Authentication
Events pertaining to authentication or authorization. SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc. These events should be of the auth or privilege metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                   | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| authmethod     | string | The method of authentication used (local, domain, LDAP, etc.) Could also include network authmethods (LANMAN, NTLMv1, NTLMv2, kerberos, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Email
Events pertaining to email or SMTP, typically from email gateways or security solutions. These events should be of the email metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                                                 | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| from           | string  | General purpose field for representing from, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP sender.  | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| mailfrom       | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mailroom designations                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| to             | string  | General purpose field for representing to, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP recipient. | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| rcptto         | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mail receipt to header designations                                                        |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| subject        | string  | Subject, with respect to communications. Typically used in email.                                                           | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| size           | integer | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                            | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |

--- Table End ---

Windows
Microsoft Windows event logs can vary greatly based on OS version, event ID, log gathering method, and other environmental factors. All types of Windows event logs should be of the windows metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy  | Type    | Description                                                                                                                                        | Notes                       |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid         | string  | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier.                                                                           | Commonly used in detection  |
| source          | string  | The source of a log event.                                                                                                                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| msg             | string  | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message.                                                                                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| logonid         | string  | Windows user login IDs which are unique between reboots on the same computer. Used to positively correlate between logins and security event logs. |                             |
| logonguid       | string  | User ID of a login identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as LogonGuid.                                                                |                             |
| process         | string  | General purpose field for storing a process name. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessName or NewProcessName.                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| pid             | integer | Any one specific process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessID or NewProcessId.                                                | Sometimes used in detection |
| pprocess        | string  | General purpose field for storing the name of a parent process. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcess.                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| ppid            | integer | Any one specific parent process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcessId.                                                   |                             |
| args            | string  | Arguments supplied to a command or operation.                                                                                                      | Commonly used in detection  |
| callingdomain   | string  | Authentication domain of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectDomainName.                                 |                             |
| callingusername | string  | Username of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserName.                                                | Commonly used in detection  |
| callinguid      | string  | User ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserSid.                                                  |                             |
| callinglogonid  | string  | Windows login ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectLogonId.                                         |                             |
| targetdomain    | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetDomainName.                                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection |
| targetusername  | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetUserName.                                                                                        | Commonly used in detection  |
| targetlogonid   | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetLogonId.                                                                                         |                             |

--- Table End ---

| antivirus       | Events generated by AV or similar host-based mechanisms (ClamAV, Symantec, Sophos, McAfee, etc.)                                                                                      |
| app_transaction | Any application based transaction activity to include application, database, or similar API transaction record                                                                        |
| auth            | Events pertaining to authentication or authorization (SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc.)                                                                                 |
| cloud           | Events pertaining to cloud infrastructure and services                                                                                                                                |
| connection      | Connection based events providing visibility of network protocols (netflow, sflow, jflow, session, connection, etc.)                                                                  |
| dhcp            | Events pertaining to Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and IP address allocation                                                                                             |
| dlp             | Events pertaining to Data Loss Prevention (DLP) or related practices                                                                                                                  |
| dns             | Events referring to any method or transaction used to interact with DNS records                                                                                                       |
| email           | Events pertaining to email message transfer (SMTP or similar logs)                                                                                                                    |
| file_xfer       | File transfers in any protocol (FTP, HTTP, SMB, BitTorrent, etc.)                                                                                                                     |
| firewall        | Connection accept/deny events generated by firewalls or similar devices which enforce ACLs on network traffic (VLAN, ACLs, etc.)                                                      |
| health          | Specialized events providing health metrics of a sensor or server                                                                                                                     |
| http_proxy      | Outbound web browsing events processed by an HTTP proxy. Includes events generated by other sources with similar content handling outgoing HTTP traffic                               |
| http_server     | Inbound web request events to a hosted web server.  Includes events generated by other sources with similar content (apache, nginx, firewalls, reverse proxies, load balancers, etc.) |
| ids             | Intrusion detection/prevention system alerts, including network (Snort, Suricata, Bro) or host-based (McAfee HIPS, OSSEC) alerts                                                      |
| nat             | Network address translation events (NAT or PAT)                                                                                                                                       |
| posix           | Events originating from POSIX, Unix, and Linux based services                                                                                                                         |
| privilege       | Events that indicate escalated user privileges(Cisco enable, sudo, runas, Windows impersonation, etc.)                                                                                |
| vpn             | VPN events from either site-to-site VPN tunnels or end user client-access VPN events                                                                                                  |
| vulnerability   | Events pertaining to vulnerability management, penetration testing, and related practices                                                                                             |
| windows         | Microsoft Windows events originating from any service in use on domain controller or workstation                                                                                      |

--- Table End ---

Commonly Used Taxonomy
General Event Information
Commonly used in many types of events.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type      | Description                                                                         | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid        | string    | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier             | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtime      | date-time | date/time that the actual event took place, as found in the payload of the message. | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtype      | string    | Type of event                                                                       | Commonly used in detection |
| msg            | string    | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Alert & Malware Information
Typically alerts from FireEye or other security products. These events may be of the antivirus or ids metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                              | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| action         | string | Action in the generic sense, typically representing action taken as a result of an event (allow, drop, quarantine, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |
| category       | string | General purpose field for Category, typically identifies a product specific category of event, alert, or activity        | Commonly used in detection |
| severity       | string | General purpose field used to capture severity level                                                                     | Commonly used in detection |
| virus          | string | General purpose field for representing the vendor specified streetname for a virus.                                      | Commonly used in detection |
| malwarename    | string | Used to represent the name of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |
| malwaretype    | string | Used to represent the type of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Network Connections
Network connections may be detailed in a variety of events including those of the connection, firewall, and http_proxy metaclasses.
Parsing should prioritize primary source and destination information including IP addresses that can be used in intel and analytics.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                          | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the source host      | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the source host      | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| srchost        | string  | Hostname of the source host          | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| srcport        | integer | Source port number                   | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| dstipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the destination host | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                      |
| dstipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the destination host | Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| dsthost        | string  | Hostname of the destination host     |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| dstport        | integer | Destination port number              | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |

--- Table End ---

VPN Connections
VPN connections should be parsed similar to other types network connections. Parsing should prioritize user and source IP/host information that can be used to detect abnormal logons. These events should be of the vpn metaclass, although it is not necessary for analytics.
HTTP Requests
HTTP requests are typically seen in events from HTTP proxies, servers, or other L7 network devices. These events should be of the http_proxy or http_server metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                          | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. May be extracted from url. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| uri            | string  | Full URI of a resource. May be extracted from url.                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| httpmethod     | string  | HTTP method (GET, POST, PUT, etc.)                                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| statuscode     | integer | HTTP status code (200, 404, 500, etc.)                                                               | Commonly used in detection                        |
| useragent      | string  | HTTP user agent string.                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |
| referrer       | string  | HTTP referrer header.                                                                                | Commonly used in detection                        |
| clientvars     | string  | Client header variables                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

DNS Requests
DNS requests are typically seen in events from DNS servers or L7 network devices. These events should be of the dns metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                               | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| querytype      | integer | A QTYPE value specifying the type of query (1, 2, 6, 12, 28, etc.)        | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| querytypename  | string  | A descriptive name for the type of query (A, NS, SOA, PTR, AAAA, etc.)    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| protocol       | string  | Protocol used in a session (http, ftp, smtp, etc.)                        | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

File Transfers
File transfers via HTTP, FTP, SMB, etc. These events should be of the file_xfer metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                                                  | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| filename       | string | General purpose field for storing a file name. May or may not include the full file path.                                                                                    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| filepath       | string | General purpose field for storing a file path.                                                                                                                               | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| hash           | string | General purpose field for storing any type of message digest hash value. Use when hashing algorithm is unknown or inconsistent. Otherwise, use md5, sha1, or sha256 instead. |                                                   |
| md5            | string | Computed MD5 hash of an object                                                                                                                                               | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha1           | string | Computed SHA1 hash of an object                                                                                                                                              | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha256         | string | Computed SHA256 hash of an object                                                                                                                                            | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| size           | string | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                                                                             | Sometimes used in detection                       |

--- Table End ---

Authentication
Events pertaining to authentication or authorization. SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc. These events should be of the auth or privilege metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                   | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| authmethod     | string | The method of authentication used (local, domain, LDAP, etc.) Could also include network authmethods (LANMAN, NTLMv1, NTLMv2, kerberos, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Email
Events pertaining to email or SMTP, typically from email gateways or security solutions. These events should be of the email metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                                                 | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| from           | string  | General purpose field for representing from, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP sender.  | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| mailfrom       | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mailroom designations                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| to             | string  | General purpose field for representing to, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP recipient. | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| rcptto         | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mail receipt to header designations                                                        |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| subject        | string  | Subject, with respect to communications. Typically used in email.                                                           | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| size           | integer | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                            | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |

--- Table End ---

Windows
Microsoft Windows event logs can vary greatly based on OS version, event ID, log gathering method, and other environmental factors. All types of Windows event logs should be of the windows metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy  | Type    | Description                                                                                                                                        | Notes                       |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid         | string  | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier.                                                                           | Commonly used in detection  |
| source          | string  | The source of a log event.                                                                                                                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| msg             | string  | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message.                                                                                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| logonid         | string  | Windows user login IDs which are unique between reboots on the same computer. Used to positively correlate between logins and security event logs. |                             |
| logonguid       | string  | User ID of a login identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as LogonGuid.                                                                |                             |
| process         | string  | General purpose field for storing a process name. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessName or NewProcessName.                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| pid             | integer | Any one specific process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessID or NewProcessId.                                                | Sometimes used in detection |
| pprocess        | string  | General purpose field for storing the name of a parent process. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcess.                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| ppid            | integer | Any one specific parent process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcessId.                                                   |                             |
| args            | string  | Arguments supplied to a command or operation.                                                                                                      | Commonly used in detection  |
| callingdomain   | string  | Authentication domain of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectDomainName.                                 |                             |
| callingusername | string  | Username of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserName.                                                | Commonly used in detection  |
| callinguid      | string  | User ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserSid.                                                  |                             |
| callinglogonid  | string  | Windows login ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectLogonId.                                         |                             |
| targetdomain    | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetDomainName.                                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection |
| targetusername  | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetUserName.                                                                                        | Commonly used in detection  |
| targetlogonid   | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetLogonId.                                                                                         |                             |

--- Table End ---

Common Taxonomy and Metaclass Usage
Metaclass Definitions
Classes in the Helix taxonomy represent types of events or log sources. A metaclass is simply a generic class name that refers to events from one or more actual classes in Helix.

--- Table Start ---

| Metaclass       | Description                                                                                                                                                                           |
|---|---|
| antivirus       | Events generated by AV or similar host-based mechanisms (ClamAV, Symantec, Sophos, McAfee, etc.)                                                                                      |
| app_transaction | Any application based transaction activity to include application, database, or similar API transaction record                                                                        |
| auth            | Events pertaining to authentication or authorization (SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc.)                                                                                 |
| cloud           | Events pertaining to cloud infrastructure and services                                                                                                                                |
| connection      | Connection based events providing visibility of network protocols (netflow, sflow, jflow, session, connection, etc.)                                                                  |
| dhcp            | Events pertaining to Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and IP address allocation                                                                                             |
| dlp             | Events pertaining to Data Loss Prevention (DLP) or related practices                                                                                                                  |
| dns             | Events referring to any method or transaction used to interact with DNS records                                                                                                       |
| email           | Events pertaining to email message transfer (SMTP or similar logs)                                                                                                                    |
| file_xfer       | File transfers in any protocol (FTP, HTTP, SMB, BitTorrent, etc.)                                                                                                                     |
| firewall        | Connection accept/deny events generated by firewalls or similar devices which enforce ACLs on network traffic (VLAN, ACLs, etc.)                                                      |
| health          | Specialized events providing health metrics of a sensor or server                                                                                                                     |
| http_proxy      | Outbound web browsing events processed by an HTTP proxy. Includes events generated by other sources with similar content handling outgoing HTTP traffic                               |
| http_server     | Inbound web request events to a hosted web server.  Includes events generated by other sources with similar content (apache, nginx, firewalls, reverse proxies, load balancers, etc.) |
| ids             | Intrusion detection/prevention system alerts, including network (Snort, Suricata, Bro) or host-based (McAfee HIPS, OSSEC) alerts                                                      |
| nat             | Network address translation events (NAT or PAT)                                                                                                                                       |
| posix           | Events originating from POSIX, Unix, and Linux based services                                                                                                                         |
| privilege       | Events that indicate escalated user privileges(Cisco enable, sudo, runas, Windows impersonation, etc.)                                                                                |
| vpn             | VPN events from either site-to-site VPN tunnels or end user client-access VPN events                                                                                                  |
| vulnerability   | Events pertaining to vulnerability management, penetration testing, and related practices                                                                                             |
| windows         | Microsoft Windows events originating from any service in use on domain controller or workstation                                                                                      |

--- Table End ---

| http_proxy      | Outbound web browsing events processed by an HTTP proxy. Includes events generated by other sources with similar content handling outgoing HTTP traffic                               |
| http_server     | Inbound web request events to a hosted web server.  Includes events generated by other sources with similar content (apache, nginx, firewalls, reverse proxies, load balancers, etc.) |
| ids             | Intrusion detection/prevention system alerts, including network (Snort, Suricata, Bro) or host-based (McAfee HIPS, OSSEC) alerts                                                      |
| nat             | Network address translation events (NAT or PAT)                                                                                                                                       |
| posix           | Events originating from POSIX, Unix, and Linux based services                                                                                                                         |
| privilege       | Events that indicate escalated user privileges(Cisco enable, sudo, runas, Windows impersonation, etc.)                                                                                |
| vpn             | VPN events from either site-to-site VPN tunnels or end user client-access VPN events                                                                                                  |
| vulnerability   | Events pertaining to vulnerability management, penetration testing, and related practices                                                                                             |
| windows         | Microsoft Windows events originating from any service in use on domain controller or workstation                                                                                      |

--- Table End ---

Commonly Used Taxonomy
General Event Information
Commonly used in many types of events.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type      | Description                                                                         | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid        | string    | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier             | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtime      | date-time | date/time that the actual event took place, as found in the payload of the message. | Commonly used in detection |
| eventtype      | string    | Type of event                                                                       | Commonly used in detection |
| msg            | string    | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Alert & Malware Information
Typically alerts from FireEye or other security products. These events may be of the antivirus or ids metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                              | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| action         | string | Action in the generic sense, typically representing action taken as a result of an event (allow, drop, quarantine, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |
| category       | string | General purpose field for Category, typically identifies a product specific category of event, alert, or activity        | Commonly used in detection |
| severity       | string | General purpose field used to capture severity level                                                                     | Commonly used in detection |
| virus          | string | General purpose field for representing the vendor specified streetname for a virus.                                      | Commonly used in detection |
| malwarename    | string | Used to represent the name of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |
| malwaretype    | string | Used to represent the type of a detected malware                                                                         | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Network Connections
Network connections may be detailed in a variety of events including those of the connection, firewall, and http_proxy metaclasses.
Parsing should prioritize primary source and destination information including IP addresses that can be used in intel and analytics.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                          | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the source host      | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the source host      | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| srchost        | string  | Hostname of the source host          | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| srcport        | integer | Source port number                   | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| dstipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the destination host | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                      |
| dstipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the destination host | Used in geo location decoration (dstisp, dstcountry, dstlatitude, dstlongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |
| dsthost        | string  | Hostname of the destination host     |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| dstport        | integer | Destination port number              | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |

--- Table End ---

VPN Connections
VPN connections should be parsed similar to other types network connections. Parsing should prioritize user and source IP/host information that can be used to detect abnormal logons. These events should be of the vpn metaclass, although it is not necessary for analytics.
HTTP Requests
HTTP requests are typically seen in events from HTTP proxies, servers, or other L7 network devices. These events should be of the http_proxy or http_server metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                          | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. May be extracted from url. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| uri            | string  | Full URI of a resource. May be extracted from url.                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| httpmethod     | string  | HTTP method (GET, POST, PUT, etc.)                                                                   | Commonly used in detection                        |
| statuscode     | integer | HTTP status code (200, 404, 500, etc.)                                                               | Commonly used in detection                        |
| useragent      | string  | HTTP user agent string.                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |
| referrer       | string  | HTTP referrer header.                                                                                | Commonly used in detection                        |
| clientvars     | string  | Client header variables                                                                              | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

DNS Requests
DNS requests are typically seen in events from DNS servers or L7 network devices. These events should be of the dns metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                               | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| domain         | string  | A domain name. Typically seen in an HTTP, DNS, or authentication request. | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| querytype      | integer | A QTYPE value specifying the type of query (1, 2, 6, 12, 28, etc.)        | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| querytypename  | string  | A descriptive name for the type of query (A, NS, SOA, PTR, AAAA, etc.)    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| protocol       | string  | Protocol used in a session (http, ftp, smtp, etc.)                        | Commonly used in detection                        |

--- Table End ---

File Transfers
File transfers via HTTP, FTP, SMB, etc. These events should be of the file_xfer metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                                                  | Notes                                             |
|---|---|---|---|
| filename       | string | General purpose field for storing a file name. May or may not include the full file path.                                                                                    | Commonly used in detection                        |
| filepath       | string | General purpose field for storing a file path.                                                                                                                               | Sometimes used in detection                       |
| hash           | string | General purpose field for storing any type of message digest hash value. Use when hashing algorithm is unknown or inconsistent. Otherwise, use md5, sha1, or sha256 instead. |                                                   |
| md5            | string | Computed MD5 hash of an object                                                                                                                                               | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha1           | string | Computed SHA1 hash of an object                                                                                                                                              | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| sha256         | string | Computed SHA256 hash of an object                                                                                                                                            | Commonly used in detection
Used in intel matching |
| size           | string | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                                                                             | Sometimes used in detection                       |

--- Table End ---

Authentication
Events pertaining to authentication or authorization. SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc. These events should be of the auth or privilege metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type   | Description                                                                                                                                   | Notes                      |
|---|---|---|---|
| authmethod     | string | The method of authentication used (local, domain, LDAP, etc.) Could also include network authmethods (LANMAN, NTLMv1, NTLMv2, kerberos, etc.) | Commonly used in detection |

--- Table End ---

Email
Events pertaining to email or SMTP, typically from email gateways or security solutions. These events should be of the email metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy | Type    | Description                                                                                                                 | Notes                                                                                                                                                                        |
|---|---|---|---|
| from           | string  | General purpose field for representing from, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP sender.  | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| mailfrom       | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mailroom designations                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| to             | string  | General purpose field for representing to, with respect to origin. Typically used in email to represent the SMTP recipient. | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| rcptto         | string  | RFC 4021 Header information, for mail receipt to header designations                                                        |                                                                                                                                                                              |
| subject        | string  | Subject, with respect to communications. Typically used in email.                                                           | Commonly used in detection                                                                                                                                                   |
| size           | integer | General purpose field for representing the size of something, e.g. disk size=2TB                                            | Sometimes used in detection                                                                                                                                                  |
| srcipv4        | IPv4    | IPv4 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Referenced in all FireEye detection rules for global exclusions
Used in intel matching
Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.) |
| srcipv6        | IPv6    | IPv6 address of the sender                                                                                                  | Used in geo location decoration (srcisp, srccountry, srclatitude, srclongitude, etc.)                                                                                        |

--- Table End ---

Windows
Microsoft Windows event logs can vary greatly based on OS version, event ID, log gathering method, and other environmental factors. All types of Windows event logs should be of the windows metaclass.

--- Table Start ---

| Helix Taxonomy  | Type    | Description                                                                                                                                        | Notes                       |
|---|---|---|---|
| eventid         | string  | General purpose field used to capture any one specific event identifier.                                                                           | Commonly used in detection  |
| source          | string  | The source of a log event.                                                                                                                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| msg             | string  | General purpose field to capture some or all of the message.                                                                                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| logonid         | string  | Windows user login IDs which are unique between reboots on the same computer. Used to positively correlate between logins and security event logs. |                             |
| logonguid       | string  | User ID of a login identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as LogonGuid.                                                                |                             |
| process         | string  | General purpose field for storing a process name. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessName or NewProcessName.                       | Commonly used in detection  |
| pid             | integer | Any one specific process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ProcessID or NewProcessId.                                                | Sometimes used in detection |
| pprocess        | string  | General purpose field for storing the name of a parent process. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcess.                         | Commonly used in detection  |
| ppid            | integer | Any one specific parent process ID. Typically observed in Windows event logs as ParentProcessId.                                                   |                             |
| args            | string  | Arguments supplied to a command or operation.                                                                                                      | Commonly used in detection  |
| callingdomain   | string  | Authentication domain of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectDomainName.                                 |                             |
| callingusername | string  | Username of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserName.                                                | Commonly used in detection  |
| callinguid      | string  | User ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectUserSid.                                                  |                             |
| callinglogonid  | string  | Windows login ID of a remote calling identity. Typically observed in Windows event logs as SubjectLogonId.                                         |                             |
| targetdomain    | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetDomainName.                                                                                      | Sometimes used in detection |
| targetusername  | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetUserName.                                                                                        | Commonly used in detection  |
| targetlogonid   | string  | Typically observed in Windows event logs as TargetLogonId.                                                                                         |                             |

--- Table End ---

Common Taxonomy and Metaclass Usage
Metaclass Definitions
Classes in the Helix taxonomy represent types of events or log sources. A metaclass is simply a generic class name that refers to events from one or more actual classes in Helix.

--- Table Start ---

| Metaclass       | Description                                                                                                                                                                           |
|---|---|
| antivirus       | Events generated by AV or similar host-based mechanisms (ClamAV, Symantec, Sophos, McAfee, etc.)                                                                                      |
| app_transaction | Any application based transaction activity to include application, database, or similar API transaction record                                                                        |
| auth            | Events pertaining to authentication or authorization (SSO, Active Directory, LDAP, RADIUS, 2FA, etc.)                                                                                 |
| cloud           | Events pertaining to cloud infrastructure and services                                                                                                                                |
| connection      | Connection based events providing visibility of network protocols (netflow, sflow, jflow, session, connection, etc.)                                                                  |
| dhcp            | Events pertaining to Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and IP address allocation                                                                                             |
| dlp             | Events pertaining to Data Loss Prevention (DLP) or related practices                                                                                                                  |
| dns             | Events referring to any method or transaction used to interact with DNS records                                                                                                       |
| email           | Events pertaining to email message transfer (SMTP or similar logs)                                                                                                                    |
| file_xfer       | File transfers in any protocol (FTP, HTTP, SMB, BitTorrent, etc.)                                                                                                                     |
| firewall        | Connection accept/deny events generated by firewalls or similar devices which enforce ACLs on network traffic (VLAN, ACLs, etc.)                                                      |
| health          | Specialized events providing health metrics of a sensor or server                                                                                                                     |
| http_proxy      | Outbound web browsing events processed by an HTTP proxy. Includes events generated by other sources with similar content handling outgoing HTTP traffic                               |
| http_server     | Inbound web request events to a hosted web server.  Includes events generated by other sources with similar content (apache, nginx, firewalls, reverse proxies, load balancers, etc.) |
| ids             | Intrusion detection/prevention system alerts, including network (Snort, Suricata, Bro) or host-based (McAfee HIPS, OSSEC) alerts                                                      |
| nat             | Network address translation events (NAT or PAT)                                                                                                                                       |
| posix           | Events originating from POSIX, Unix, and Linux based services                                                                                                                         |
| privilege       | Events that indicate escalated user privileges(Cisco enable, sudo, runas, Windows impersonation, etc.)                                                                                |
| vpn             | VPN events from either site-to-site VPN tunnels or end user client-access VPN events                                                                                                  |
| vulnerability   | Events pertaining to vulnerability management, penetration testing, and related practices                                                                                             |
| windows         | Microsoft Windows events originating from any service in use on domain controller or workstation                                                                                      |

--- Table End ---
